SAMPLE     Targets were mounted in aluminium frames with 25 mm    D030200100014 
           diameter apertures, which again were mounted on an     D030200100015 
           aluminium target ladder that fits onto a target        D030200100016 
           drive mechanism at the centre of the large NAC         D030200100017 
           scattering chamber.                                    D030200100018 
METHOD     (EDE,COINC)                                            D030200100019 
PART-DET   (A)                                                    D030200100020 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SISD,NAICR) Two detector telescopes were mountedD030200100021 
           on rotatable arms on opposite sides of the beam axis,  D030200100022 
           in the same reaction plane. Each telescope consisted ofD030200100023 
           a single doublesided SSD as a dE detector, followed by D030200100024 
           a single NaI stopping E detector.                      D030200100025 
           The SSD have 16 vertical anode strips and 16 horizontalD030200100026 
           cathode strips each, with an active area of            D030200100027 
           50 mm x 50 mm. The inter-strip gaps are 100 mu-min     D030200100028 
           width. Several detector thicknesses were utilized,     D030200100029 
           depending on the incident beam energy. (See SUBENTs).  D030200100030 
           The stopping detectors used have NaI(Tl) crystals of   D030200100031 
           3 inch in diam. and 2 inch thickness.                  D030200100032 
EN-SEC     (E-LVL,4-BE-8)                                         D030200100033 
           (E,4-BE-8)                                             D030200100034
